  var currentBreakpoint;
  var defaultSelector = '[data-height-xs]';
  var elements = document.querySelectorAll(defaultSelector);
  var breakpoints = [0, 768, 992, 1200];
  var sizes = ['xs', 'sm', 'md', 'lg'];

  function getCurrentBreakpoint() {
    var length = breakpoints.length;
    var windowWidth = window.innerWidth;

    for(var i = 0; i &lt; length; i++){
      var breakpoint = breakpoints[i];
      if(breakpoint &lt;= windowWidth) {
        size = i;
      }
    }

    return size;
  }

  function setSizes() {
    var length = elements.length;
    var breakpointAttributeToUse;
    currentBreakpoint = getCurrentBreakpoint();

    for(var i = 0; i &lt; length; i++){
      var dataAttributes = [].filter.call(elements[i].attributes, function(attribute) {
        return attribute.nodeName.indexOf('data-height-') !== -1;
      });

      dataAttributes.every(function(attribute, index) {
        if(attribute.nodeName === 'data-height-' + sizes[currentBreakpoint] || (index + 1) === dataAttributes.length) {
          breakpointAttributeToUse = attribute;
          return false;
        }

        return true;
      });
      
      var height = elements[i].getAttribute(breakpointAttributeToUse.nodeName);
      elements[i].style.display = 'block';
      elements[i].style.height = height + 'px';
    }
  }

  window.addEventListener('resize', function(){
    if(currentBreakpoint !== getCurrentBreakpoint()) {
      setSizes();
    }
  });

  setSizes();
  window.lazySizesConfig = window.lazySizesConfig || {};
  window.lazySizesConfig.srcAttr = 'data-source';

  document.addEventListener('lazyloaded', function(e){
